RATING: 7
[b]A RIGHT GOOD ZOMBIE-KILLING ROMP IN GLORIOUS B-MOVIE TRADITION, FEATURING PUMP-ACTION SHOTGUNS & BUZZING CHAINSAWS![/b]

I really like this game. It's a tile-laying, card-playing, dice-rolling action game, that doesn't take itself very seriously. But it is a toolkit. Accept it. I would score this a 5 or a 6 if I was using the clunky, confusing official rules bundled with the box. We only ever play using my house rules - the rules out of the box stink like zombie-flesh; dragging the game into the small hours if played with 4+ gamers, especially with arguments started over timing issues caused by the ill-worded, but fantastically illustrated, event cards. This should not put players off, because the theme is so great, and the rules so easy to change, that it is worth persevering with this little gem. Even the game's designers admit that Zombies, out of the box, is the seed that can be planted to grow into your own style of game system. We have always had FUN playing this game, and that's the main aim of boardgaming, isn't it? But, boy, does this game take a battering to the head, with a blood-stained cricket bat, on the Geek! 

If you like zombie movies and the Resident Evil videogames, then this game can suit your needs. The premise is simple, like most cool, zombie flicks: some dudes are in imminent danger of having the flesh ripped from their bones by hordes of lurching zombies, and must fight to get to a helicopter and escape. Screwing over the other players on the way is a good strategy and also a chucklesome pastime.

[b]Q: How does this compare to Last Night on Earth?[/b]
[b]A:[/b] Okay. LNoE has superior production values, gimmicky photoshopped cards, and also great big tileboards. That's all fine and dandy. However, Zombies has the better themic fit for my money. Urban zombie scenarios always trump zombie farmhands attacking steadings, IMHO. How many zombie flicks feature farms over, say, a mall? Not many. I have a fondness for building up a doomed town and exploring on the run, rather than having it all laid out at the beginning. You lose that "what's coming up next?" factor. Zombies also has the better artwork on the cards. Fact.

[i]Having said all that, to really enjoy this game do the following polishes:[/i]

1. Throw out the rulebook.
2. Pick and choose from the variant rules on the Geek - remember to keep it SIMPLE!
3. Do not lay down tiles after finding the helipad.
4. Forget counting "dead" zombies for the winner - this is a kill-the-zombie-to-escape game. Let the most bloodthirst player place the helipad.
5. When a player dies, have him/her/them control the zombies, etc.
6. Trim the card deck to a custom-picked 50-60 cards. NO more, no less. Keep it 50/50 to screwage/benefit cards.
7. Use a timer - this keeps a panicky atmosphere ticking over.
8. Mount the town tiles on 2mm-thick card.
9. Use the subway expansion.

We also feature bosses like RE's Nemesis to spice up the challenge, sometimes. I also bought a set of REAL 9mm bullets to replace the tokens - talk about game-pimping!

The game is a blast with the right crowd. It can also be a breath of fresh air after playing El Grande or Puerto Rico. BRAINNSSS!

[b]Tips for the game designers to ignore:[/b]

1. Keep the artist: he's brilliant.
2. Keep the deep game-box.
3. Hire someone to rewrite the rules, and the fuzzy wordage on the cards.
4. Have the tiles made of thicker card.

RATING: 5
I didn't have high expectations prior to playing this game, because TC has a reputation to produce games that are extremely awkward, incomplete, etc.  This game though is definitely fun, albeit random, but I enjoyed it each time I played it - this was a pleasant surprise!

The components are what to be expected as all TC games are virtually the same in regards to components.  They are pretty well done and very durable.  I like the artwork in this game.

The gameplay, as I mentioned, can be redundant and definitely random!  Since your success highly relies upon die rolls, luck is a major issue here.  There will always be those players that roll extremely well and those who do not... this is to be expected.

Prior to playing the game, I already knew what to expect and so taking all into account, I did enjoy playing Zombies!!!  I am very happy to add it into my ever-growing collection and it is a well-welcomed addition!

RATING: 8
I have this and a few of the expansions, but I can't remember which ones. Zombies!!! actually came out like, slightly ahead of the huge Zombie cultural obsession curve. 

It's a tile-based dungeon crawl (or survival-horror crawl, I guess) to gain supplies and get to the helipad to win. You can help or harm other players as you like, or as gameplay dictates. 

It's been a LONG time since I've played this. It's an old game so it's kind of fallen out of popularity, which is a shame. It's still super fun. Plays 4 or 5 players - maybe more with the expansions. One of the expansions has glow-in-the-dark irradiated zombies, and I think another has zombie dogs.

=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
RATING: 5.9
[imageid=1611677 small]

Standard roll and move affair with a handful of nicely illustrated cards thrown into the mix which spice up the proceedings.

Basically, land on a square with a zombie and kill it on a roll of 4-6. Kill 25 of these, or reach a helicopter pad and you win.

Most of the cards are difficult to bring into play, as you need to be in a certain location to acquire them, and a few of the cards are open to interpretation due to poor wording and a lacking rulebook. But nail down most of these issues and you'll at least get some fun out of it. Just don't expect an in-depth game where you need to exercise your noggin.

RATING: 5
I own this and most the expansions, and I love it. Been playing this game for years. But getting it to the table is a feat of strength in itself. Never have i Played a game that gets blood boiling so quickly, forces people to stew in selfishness and hatred so deeply. Bring your hate game because arguments will happen and tempers will get elevated. I love every minute of it, but those I play with don't, so a 5 because no one will play with me.

P.S. the arguments can get heated and brutally stupid-mean, but once victory is claimed by someone it all seems to go away, so it isn't long lasted, just detested in the moment. Enjoy!
